COMMENT    The spectra of photoprotons from the S-32 nucleus are  M0045  1   19 
            measured in the bremsstrahlung beam. The upper limit  M0045  1   20 
            of the bremsstrahlung spectrum was varied from 17 to  M0045  1   21 
            30 MeV in shorter than 1-MeV steps. The spectra are   M0045  1   22 
            used to calculate the distribution of transition to   M0045  1   23 
            different states of the residual nucleus P-31 and to  M0045  1   24 
            determine the corresponding partial photoproton cross M0045  1   25 
            section.                                              M0045  1   26
